#### <blank>  

#### For the the "keybinds" in the main menu (e.g. ggh for github) please add code that highlights each character of the keybind as it's pressed. (e.g. i press g, the keybinds that start with g highlight the g). if the user enters a full keybind it should automatically navigate them to that link. when a user presses a key it may put them into "insert mode" exiting insert mode should clear any previously typed characters  

Okay, this is a complex request that will require changes in multiple files. Here's a breakdown of the necessary steps and the code modifications:

**1. Update `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**

   - Add state to track the currently pressed keys for the keybind.
   - Modify the keydown event listener to capture key presses and update the state.
   - Add logic to check if a full keybind has been entered and navigate accordingly.
   - Add logic to clear the pressed keys when exiting insert mode.

```svelte
// src/routes/+layout.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import { injectSpeedInsights } from '@vercel/speed-insights/sveltekit';
	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';
	import { browser } from '$app/environment';
	import '../app.css';
	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			const keybinds = {
				github: 'ggh',
				twitter: 'gx',
				twitch: 'gt',
				youtube: 'gyt',
				linkedin: 'gli',
				talks: 'gct',
				email: 'gcm'
			};

			const linkMap = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
```

**2. Update `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**

   - Add a `pressedKeys` prop.
   - Modify the display of the keybinds to highlight matching characters.

```svelte
// src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="font-bold">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main
	id="main"
	class="flex flex-col mx-auto mt-16 gap-5 items-center text-ctp-text"
>
	<Ascii />
	<p class="text-center lg:text-3xl text-xl text-ctp-crust bg-mode-color p-3">
		software engineer @ vercel ‚ñ≤
	</p>
	<ul
		class="flex flex-col lg:w-1/2 w-3/4 gap-2 lg:mt-8 mt-2 mb-8 lg:text-[22px] text-base"
	>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="github"
				class="flex group/link flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://github.com/dmmulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><Github
						class="group-hover:text-[#2dba4e] group-focus/link:text-[#2dba4e]"
					/>GitHub</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('ggh', pressedKeys)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="twitter"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"

					/>Twitch</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gt', pressedKeys)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="youtube"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"

**3. Update `src/routes/+page.svelte`:**

   - Pass the `pressedKeys` state to the `MainMenu` component.

```svelte
// src/routes/+page.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import MainMenu from './main-menu.svelte';
	import { getContext } from 'svelte';

	const pressedKeys = getContext('pressedKeys');
</script>

<MainMenu pressedKeys={$pressedKeys} />
```

**4. Update `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**

   - Add `setContext` to pass the `pressedKeys` state to the `+page.svelte` component.

```svelte
// src/routes/+layout.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import { injectSpeedInsights } from '@vercel/speed-insights/sveltekit';
	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';
	import { browser } from '$app/environment';
	import '../app.css';
	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	import { setContext } from 'svelte';
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys

		setContext('pressedKeys', { subscribe: () => ({}) });

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			const keybinds = {
				github: 'ggh',
				twitter: 'gx',
				twitch: 'gt',
				youtube: 'gyt',
				linkedin: 'gli',
				talks: 'gct',
				email: 'gcm'
			};

			const linkMap = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
```

**5. Install `svelte` as a dev dependency**

```bash
bun add -d svelte
```

**Explanation:**

-   **`src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**
    -   `pressedKeys`: This state variable stores the sequence of keys pressed by the user.
    -   The `keydown` event listener now captures all key presses when in NORMAL mode.
    -   It checks if the pressed keys match a full keybind. If so, it navigates to the corresponding URL.
    -   The `pressedKeys` variable is cleared when entering or exiting INSERT/VISUAL mode, or when a full keybind is matched.
-   **`src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**
    -   The `highlightKeybind` function iterates through the keybind string and wraps each character that matches the `pressedKeys` in a `<span>` with a `font-bold` class.  This will highlight the matching characters.
    -   `{@html ...}` is used to render the highlighted keybinds as HTML.
-   **`src/routes/+page.svelte`:**
    -   The `pressedKeys` state is passed to the `MainMenu` component.
-   **`src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**
    -   The `pressedKeys` state is passed to the `+page.svelte` component using `setContext`.

**CSS (Optional):**

You can add the following CSS to `src/app.css` to style the highlighted characters:

```css
/* src/app.css */
.font-bold {
  color: var(--ctp-rose); /* Or any color you prefer */
}
```

This should provide the desired highlighting effect and navigation. Remember to test thoroughly!

> src/app.css  
> Add file to the chat? (Y)es/(N)o/(D)on't ask again [Yes]: y  

Thanks for providing the `src/app.css` file. I've reviewed the changes and noticed a potential issue. The CSS provided defines a `.font-bold` class, but it might not be specific enough to only target the highlighted keybinds within the `MainMenu` component. This could lead to unintended styling of other elements with the same class.

To avoid this, I recommend modifying the `highlightKeybind` function in `src/routes/main-menu.svelte` to use a more specific class name.

**Modification to `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main
	id="main"
	class="flex flex-col mx-auto mt-16 gap-5 items-center text-ctp-text"
>
	<Ascii />
	<p class="text-center lg:text-3xl text-xl text-ctp-crust bg-mode-color p-3">
		software engineer @ vercel ‚ñ≤
	</p>
	<ul
		class="flex flex-col lg:w-1/2 w-3/4 gap-2 lg:mt-8 mt-2 mb-8 lg:text-[22px] text-base"
	>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="github"
				class="flex group/link flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://github.com/dmmulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><Github
						class="group-hover:text-[#2dba4e] group-focus/link:text-[#2dba4e]"
					/>GitHub</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('ggh', pressedKeys)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="twitter"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://x.com/dillon_mulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><TwitterIcon
						class="group-hover:text-[#1D9BF0] group-focus/link:text-[#1D9BF0]"
					/>Twitter/ùïè</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gx', pressedKeys)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="twitch"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><TwitchIcon
						class="group-hover:text-[#6441a5] group-focus/link:text-[#6441a5]"
					/>Twitch</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gt', pressedKeys)}</a
			>
		</li>

			<a
				id="youtube"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://youtube.com/dmmulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"

```css
/* src/app.css */
@tailwind base;

:root {
	--mode-color: rgb(var(--ctp-blue));

	background-color: rgb(var(--ctp-base));
}

.keybind-highlight {
  font-weight: bold;
  color: var(--ctp-rose); /* Or any color you prefer */
}

By using a more specific class name (`keybind-highlight`), we ensure that only the highlighted keybinds are affected by the CSS rule.

#### Thanks for providing the `src/app.css` file. I've reviewed the changes and noticed a potential issue. The CSS provided defines a `.font-bold` class, but it might not be specific enough to only target the highlighted keybinds within the `MainMenu` component. This could lead to unintended styling of other elements with the same class.  
####   
#### To avoid this, I recommend modifying the `highlightKeybind` function in `src/routes/main-menu.svelte` to use a more specific class name.  
####

	} from 'lucide-svelte';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

The application is throwing a 500 Internal Error. This is likely due to the changes made earlier. The error message on the page isn't very helpful, so let's start debugging.

Based on the previous changes, the most likely cause of the error is in `src/routes/+layout.svelte` or `src/routes/+page.svelte` where the `pressedKeys` context is being used.

Here's what we'll do:

1.  **Examine `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:** The `setContext` call is likely the culprit. It's currently setting the context to an empty object with a `subscribe` method. This is incorrect. It should be a writable store.

2.  **Modify `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:** Import `writable` from `svelte/store` and use it to create a store for `pressedKeys`.

3.  **Modify `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:** Update the `setContext` call to pass the `pressedKeys` store.

4.  **Modify `src/routes/+page.svelte`:** Get the `pressedKeys` store from the context and subscribe to it.

Here are the code changes:

**1. Modify `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/+layout.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import { injectSpeedInsights } from '@vercel/speed-insights/sveltekit';
	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';
	import { browser } from '$app/environment';
	import '../app.css';
	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	import { setContext } from 'svelte';
	import { writable } from 'svelte/store'; // Import writable
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys
		const pressedKeysStore = writable(''); // Create a writable store

		setContext('pressedKeys', pressedKeysStore); // Pass the store to the context

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			const keybinds = {
				github: 'ggh',
				twitter: 'gx',
				twitch: 'gt',
				youtube: 'gyt',
				linkedin: 'gli',
				talks: 'gct',
				email: 'gcm'
			};

			const linkMap = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode
				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;
				pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys); // Update the store

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
```

**2. Modify `src/routes/+page.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/+page.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import MainMenu from './main-menu.svelte';
	import { getContext } from 'svelte';
	import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	const pressedKeys = getContext<Writable<string>>('pressedKeys');
</script>

<svelte:head>
	<title>dillonis.online</title>
	<meta name="description" content="Dillon Mulroy's personal website" />
</svelte:head>

<MainMenu pressedKeys={$pressedKeys} />
```

**Explanation:**

*   **`src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**
    *   Imported `writable` from `svelte/store`.
    *   Created a `pressedKeysStore` using `writable('')`.
    *   Updated `setContext` to pass the `pressedKeysStore`.
    *   Call `pressedKeysStore.set('')` to clear the store.
    *   Call `pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys)` to update the store.
*   **`src/routes/+page.svelte`:**
    *   The `pressedKeys` context is now correctly retrieved as a writable store.
    *   The `pressedKeys` prop is passed to the `MainMenu` component.

These changes should resolve the 500 error and allow the `MainMenu` component to reactively update based on the pressed keys.

```svelte

	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				return;
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div

>

			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode
				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;
				pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys); // Update the store

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
>>>>>>> REPLACE
```

The error message `TypeError: Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'length')` in `src/routes/main-menu.svelte` indicates that `pressedKeys` is undefined when `highlightKeybind` is called.

Looking at `src/routes/+page.svelte`, `pressedKeys` is obtained from the context, and it's expected to be a store. However, in `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`, the component expects `pressedKeys` to be a string, not a store. It then tries to access the `length` property of this string.

To fix this, we need to access the value of the `pressedKeys` store in `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`.

**Modify `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  import { get } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: { subscribe: (arg0: (value: string) => void) => void; };
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  $: pressedKeysValue = get(pressedKeys);

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeysValue: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeysValue.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeysValue[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main

	class="flex flex-col mx-auto mt-16 gap-5 items-center text-ctp-text"

			>
		</li>
	</ul>
</main>

**Explanation:**

*   **`src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**
    *   Imported `get` from `svelte/store`.
    *   Updated the type definition of the `pressedKeys` prop to be a store.
    *   Used `get(pressedKeys)` to get the current value of the store and assign it to `pressedKeysValue`.
    *   Passed `pressedKeysValue` to the `highlightKeybind` function.

These changes should resolve the TypeError and allow the highlighting to work correctly.

#### **Explanation:**  
####   
#### *   **`src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**  
####     *   Imported `get` from `svelte/store`.  
####     *   Updated the type definition of the `pressedKeys` prop to be a store.  
####     *   Used `get(pressedKeys)` to get the current value of the store and assign it to `pressedKeysValue`.  
####     *   Passed `pressedKeysValue` to the `highlightKeybind` function.  
####   
#### These changes should resolve the TypeError and allow the highlighting to work correctly.  

```
src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<<<<<<< SEARCH
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main
	id="main"

		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  import { get } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: { subscribe: (arg0: (value: string) => void) => void; };
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  $: pressedKeysValue = get(pressedKeys);

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeysValue: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeysValue.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeysValue[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

> Tokens: 11k sent, 2.5k received. Cost: $0.0021 message, $0.02 session.  
> Applied edit to src/routes/main-menu.svelte  

#### check localhost  

After reviewing the code again, I see a potential issue in how the `pressedKeys` store is being accessed in `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`.

Currently, you're using `get(pressedKeys)` within the component's script to get the value of the store. This approach calculates `pressedKeysValue` only once when the component is initialized. It won't reactively update when the `pressedKeys` store changes.

To fix this, you should use the `$`: syntax to create a reactive declaration that automatically updates `pressedKeysValue` whenever the `pressedKeys` store changes.

**Modify `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  import { get } from 'svelte/store';
  import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: Writable<string>;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys;

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeysValue: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeysValue.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeysValue[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main
	id="main"
	class="flex flex-col mx-auto mt-16 gap-5 items-center text-ctp-text"
>
	<Ascii />
	<p class="text-center lg:text-3xl text-xl text-ctp-crust bg-mode-color p-3">
		software engineer @ vercel ‚ñ≤
	</p>
	<ul
		class="flex flex-col lg:w-1/2 w-3/4 gap-2 lg:mt-8 mt-2 mb-8 lg:text-[22px] text-base"
	>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="github"
				class="flex group/link flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://github.com/dmmulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><Github
						class="group-hover:text-[#2dba4e] group-focus/link:text-[#2dba4e]"
					/>GitHub</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('ggh', pressedKeysValue)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="twitter"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://x.com/dillon_mulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><TwitterIcon
						class="group-hover:text-[#1D9BF0] group-focus/link:text-[#1D9BF0]"
					/>Twitter/ùïè</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gx', pressedKeysValue)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="twitch"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><TwitchIcon
						class="group-hover:text-[#6441a5] group-focus/link:text-[#6441a5]"
					/>Twitch</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gt', pressedKeysValue)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="youtube"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://youtube.com/dmmulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><YoutubeIcon
						class="group-hover:text-[#FF1A1A] group-focus/link:text-[#FF1A1A]"
					/>YouTube</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gyt', pressedKeysValue)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="linkedin"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><LinkedinIcon
						class="group-hover:text-[#0a66c2] group-focus/link:text-[#0a66c2]"
					/>LinkedIn</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gli', pressedKeysValue)}
			</a>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="talks"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://dillonis.online/talks"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><MicVocalIcon
						class="group-hover:text-ctp-peach group-focus/link:text-ctp-peach "
					/>Conference Talks</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gct', pressedKeysValue)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="email"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><MailPlusIcon
						class="group-hover:text-ctp-mauve group-focus/link:text-ctp-mauve"
					/>Contact Me</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gcm', pressedKeysValue)}</a
			>
		</li>
	</ul>
</main>

**Explanation:**

*   **`src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**
    *   The type definition of the `pressedKeys` prop is updated to `Writable<string>`.
    *   Replaced `$: pressedKeysValue = get(pressedKeys)` with `$: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys`. This makes `pressedKeysValue` a reactive declaration, so it automatically updates whenever the value of the `pressedKeys` store changes.

These changes should ensure that the highlighting updates in real-time as the user types.

> Tokens: 16k sent, 1.7k received. Cost: $0.0023 message, $0.02 session.  
> Edit the files? (Y)es/(N)o [Yes]: n  

#### We are using svelte 5, not 4. Please review the docs at https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/overview and https://svelte.dev/docs/kit/introduction please make any neccessary changes to use svelte 5  
> https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/overview

> https://svelte.dev/docs/kit/introduction  
> Add URL to the chat? (Y)es/(N)o/(A)ll/(S)kip all/(D)on't ask again [Yes]: y  
> Scraping https://svelte.dev/docs/kit/introduction...  

Thanks for the links to the Svelte 5 documentation. I've reviewed the code and identified the necessary changes to align with Svelte 5's runes.

Here's a breakdown of the changes:

1.  **Remove `svelte/store` imports and usage:** Svelte 5 introduces runes, which replace the need for external store libraries like `svelte/store` for simple state management.

2.  **Use `$state` for `pressedKeys` in `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**  The `pressedKeys` variable should be a state variable.

3.  **Use `$state` for `tildes` in `src/routes/sign-column.svelte`:** The `tildes` variable should be a state variable.

4.  **Remove `get` from `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:** The `get` function is no longer needed.

5.  **Update `Props` type in `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:** The `Props` type should reflect that `pressedKeys` is now a string, not a store.

Here are the code modifications:

**1. Modify `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/+layout.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import { injectSpeedInsights } from '@vercel/speed-insights/sveltekit';
	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';
	import { browser } from '$app/environment';
	import '../app.css';
	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	import { setContext } from 'svelte';
	// import { writable } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove writable import
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys
		// const pressedKeysStore = writable(''); // Create a writable store

		setContext('pressedKeys', pressedKeys); // Pass the state to the context

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			const keybinds = {
				github: 'ggh',
				twitter: 'gx',
				twitch: 'gt',
				youtube: 'gyt',
				linkedin: 'gli',
				talks: 'gct',
				email: 'gcm'
			};

			const linkMap = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;
				// pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys); // Update the store

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
```

**2. Modify `src/routes/+page.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/+page.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import MainMenu from './main-menu.svelte';
	import { getContext } from 'svelte';
	// import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	const pressedKeys = getContext<string>('pressedKeys');
</script>

<svelte:head>
	<title>dillonis.online</title>
	<meta name="description" content="Dillon Mulroy's personal website" />
</svelte:head>

<MainMenu pressedKeys={pressedKeys} />
```

**3. Modify `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**

	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  // import { get } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove get import
  import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys;

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];

		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode

					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();

				pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;

Thanks for providing the error message and the link to the Svelte documentation.

The error message `ReferenceError: pressedKeysValue is not defined` indicates that `pressedKeysValue` is not accessible within the scope where it's being used. This is because we removed the reactive declaration `$: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys` in the previous step, but we're still referencing `pressedKeysValue` in the template.

To fix this, we should directly use the `pressedKeys` variable (which now holds the string value) in the `highlightKeybind` function and in the template.

**Modify `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  // import { get } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove get import
  import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys; // Remove reactive declaration

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main
	id="main"
	class="flex flex-col mx-auto mt-16 gap-5 items-center text-ctp-text"
>
	<Ascii />
	<p class="text-center lg:text-3xl text-xl text-ctp-crust bg-mode-color p-3">

	</p>

				target="_blank"

					/>Conference Talks</span

		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="email"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"

				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><MailPlusIcon
						class="group-hover:text-ctp-mauve group-focus/link:text-ctp-mauve"

```

Additionally, the warning `src/routes/+layout.svelte:18:28 State referenced in its own scope will never update. Did you mean to reference it inside a closure?` indicates that the `pressedKeys` state variable is being referenced in its own scope, which can lead to unexpected behavior.

To address this, we can wrap the `setContext` call in a function, as suggested by the warning message. This ensures that the context is updated whenever the `pressedKeys` value changes.

**Modify `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**

```svelte
// src/routes/+layout.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import { injectSpeedInsights } from '@vercel/speed-insights/sveltekit';
	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';
	import { browser } from '$app/environment';
	import '../app.css';
	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	import { setContext } from 'svelte';
	// import { writable } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove writable import
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys
		// const pressedKeysStore = writable(''); // Create a writable store

		setContext('pressedKeys', () => pressedKeys); // Pass the state to the context

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			const keybinds = {
				github: 'ggh',
				twitter: 'gx',
				twitch: 'gt',
				youtube: 'gyt',
				linkedin: 'gli',
				talks: 'gct',
				email: 'gcm'
			};

			const linkMap = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;
				// pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys); // Update the store

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
```

With these changes, the code should now be compatible with Svelte 5, utilize runes for state management, and address the `ReferenceError` and the `state_referenced_locally` warning.

> Tokens: 34k sent, 3.0k received. Cost: $0.0046 message, $0.03 session.  
> Edit the files? (Y)es/(N)o [Yes]: y  

#### Thanks for providing the error message and the link to the Svelte documentation.  
####   
#### The error message `ReferenceError: pressedKeysValue is not defined` indicates that `pressedKeysValue` is not accessible within the scope where it's being used. This is because we removed the reactive declaration `$: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys` in the previous step, but we're still referencing `pressedKeysValue` in the template.  
####   
#### To fix this, we should directly use the `pressedKeys` variable (which now holds the string value) in the `highlightKeybind` function and in the template.  
####   
#### **Modify `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**  
####   
#### ```svelte  
#### // src/routes/main-menu.svelte  
#### <script lang="ts">  
#### 	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';  
#### 	import {  
#### 		Github,  
#### 		LinkedinIcon,  
#### 		MailPlusIcon,  
#### 		MicVocalIcon,  
#### 		TwitchIcon,  
#### 		TwitterIcon,  
#### 		YoutubeIcon  
#### 	} from 'lucide-svelte';  
####   // import { get } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove get import  
####   import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';  
####   
#### 	type Props = {  
#### 		pressedKeys: string;  
#### 	};  
####   
#### 	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();  
####   
####   // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys; // Remove reactive declaration  
####   
#### 	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {  
#### 		let highlighted = '';  
#### 		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {  
#### 			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {  
#### 				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;  
#### 			} else {  
#### 				highlighted += keybind[i];  
#### 			}  
#### 		}  
#### 		return highlighted;  
#### 	}  
#### </script>

#### 				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(  
#### 					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys  
#### 				);  
####   
#### 				if (fullKeybind) {  
#### 					// Navigate if full keybind is entered  
#### 					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];  
#### 					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation  
#### 					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store  
#### 					return;  
#### 				}  
#### 			}  
#### 		});  
#### 	}  
####   
#### 	injectSpeedInsights();  
#### </script>  
####   
#### <div  
#### 	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"  
#### >  
#### 	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">  
#### 		<SignColumn />  
#### 		{@render children()}  
#### 	</div>  
#### 	<StatusLine />  
#### </div>  
#### ```  
####   
#### With these changes, the code should now be compatible with Svelte 5, utilize runes for state management, and address the `ReferenceError` and the `state_referenced_locally` warning.

	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys;

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

**Explanation of Changes:**

*   **src/routes/main-menu.svelte:**
    *   Replaced `pressedKeysValue` with `pressedKeys` in the `highlightKeybind` function calls.
    *   Removed the reactive declaration `$: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys`.
*   **src/routes/+page.svelte:**
    *   Updated the `getContext` call to reflect that it now returns a function (`() => string`).
    *   Called the `pressedKeys` context value as a function: `pressedKeys={$pressedKeys()}`.

These changes should resolve the `ReferenceError` and ensure that the `pressedKeys` value is correctly passed and used in the `MainMenu` component.

	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys;

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

```
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  // import { get } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove get import
  import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys;

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

You're absolutely right! I apologize for the oversight. I missed a crucial step in the previous correction.

Looking at the current code for `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`, I see that I removed the reactive declaration `$: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys`, but I *didn't* update the template to use the `pressedKeys` prop directly. Instead, it's still trying to reference the undefined `pressedKeysValue`.

I also see that I reverted the change to `setContext` in `src/routes/+layout.svelte`.

Here's the corrected `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:

```svelte
// src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main
	id="main"
	class="flex flex-col mx-auto mt-16 gap-5 items-center text-ctp-text"
>

	<p class="text-center lg:text-3xl text-xl text-ctp-crust bg-mode-color p-3">
		software engineer @ vercel ‚ñ≤

			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="linkedin"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><LinkedinIcon
						class="group-hover:text-[#0a66c2] group-focus/link:text-[#0a66c2]"
					/>LinkedIn</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gli', pressedKeys)}
			</a>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="talks"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="https://dillonis.online/talks"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><MicVocalIcon
						class="group-hover:text-ctp-peach group-focus/link:text-ctp-peach "
					/>Conference Talks</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gct', pressedKeys)}</a
			>
		</li>
		<li class="group cursor-none hover:cursor-pointer">
			<a
				id="email"
				class="group/link flex flex-row h-full w-full p-2 focus:outline-none focus:bg-[#313346] gap-2 items-center justify-between hover:bg-[#313346]"
				href="mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com"
				target="_blank"
			>
				<span class="flex flex-row gap-4 items-center"
					><MailPlusIcon
						class="group-hover:text-ctp-mauve group-focus/link:text-ctp-mauve"
					/>Contact Me</span
				>{@html highlightKeybind('gcm', pressedKeys)}</a
			>
		</li>
	</ul>
</main>
```

And here's the corrected `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:

```svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import { injectSpeedInsights } from '@vercel/speed-insights/sveltekit';
	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';
	import { browser } from '$app/environment';
	import '../app.css';
	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	import { setContext } from 'svelte';
	// import { writable } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove writable import
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys
		// const pressedKeysStore = writable(''); // Create a writable store

		setContext('pressedKeys', () => pressedKeys); // Pass the state to the context

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			const keybinds = {
				github: 'ggh',
				twitter: 'gx',
				twitch: 'gt',
				youtube: 'gyt',
				linkedin: 'gli',
				talks: 'gct',
				email: 'gcm'
			};

			const linkMap = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;
				// pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys); // Update the store

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
```

Please apply these changes, and the error should be resolved. I apologize again for the previous mistake.

Looking at the file contents you provided, there are Git merge conflict markers (`<<<<<<< SEARCH`, `>>>>>>> REVISED`, etc.) present in both `src/routes/main-menu.svelte` and `src/routes/+layout.svelte`. These markers are invalid syntax and need to be removed.

**1. Modify `src/routes/main-menu.svelte`:**

   - Remove the merge conflict markers (`>>>>>>> REVISED`, ````, `src/routes/+layout.svelte`, ````svelte`, `<<<<<<< SEARCH`, etc.) at the end of the file.
   - Ensure the final `{@html highlightKeybind('gcm', pressedKeys)}` call uses `pressedKeys` and not `pressedKeysValue`.

```svelte
// src/routes/main-menu.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  // import { get } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove get import
  import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys;

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

<main
	id="main"
	class="flex flex-col mx-auto mt-16 gap-5 items-center text-ctp-text"
>

**2. Modify `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:**

   - Remove the merge conflict markers (`<<<<<<< SEARCH`) around the `setContext` line.
   - Ensure the `setContext` call is `setContext('pressedKeys', () => pressedKeys);`.

```svelte
// src/routes/+layout.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import { injectSpeedInsights } from '@vercel/speed-insights/sveltekit';
	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';
	import { browser } from '$app/environment';
	import '../app.css';
	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';
	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';
	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';
	import { setContext } from 'svelte';
	// import { writable } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove writable import
	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();

	if (browser) {
		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys
		// const pressedKeysStore = writable(''); // Create a writable store

		setContext('pressedKeys', () => pressedKeys); // Pass the state to the context

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');
			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');
			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');
			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');
			const email = document.getElementById('email');

			const menuItems = [
				github,
				twitter,
				twitch,
				youtube,
				linkedin,
				talks,
				email
			];

			const keybinds = {
				github: 'ggh',
				twitter: 'gx',
				twitch: 'gt',
				youtube: 'gyt',
				linkedin: 'gli',
				talks: 'gct',
				email: 'gcm'
			};

			const linkMap = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!talks ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('INSERT');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {
				setMode('NORMAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store

				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
				}
				setMode('VISUAL');
				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode
				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
				return;
			}

			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {
				pressedKeys += event.key;
				// pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys); // Update the store

				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(
					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys
				);

				if (fullKeybind) {
					// Navigate if full keybind is entered
					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];
					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation
					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store
					return;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	injectSpeedInsights();
</script>

<div
	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"
>
	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">
		<SignColumn />
		{@render children()}
	</div>
	<StatusLine />
</div>
```

**3. Modify `src/routes/+page.svelte`:**

   - The `getContext` call should return a function that returns the string. You need to call this function to get the actual string value.

```svelte
// src/routes/+page.svelte
<script lang="ts">
	import MainMenu from './main-menu.svelte';
	import { getContext } from 'svelte';
	// import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	const getPressedKeys = getContext<() => string>('pressedKeys');
</script>

<svelte:head>
	<title>dillonis.online</title>
	<meta name="description" content="Dillon Mulroy's personal website" />
</svelte:head>

<MainMenu pressedKeys={getPressedKeys()} />
```

These changes remove the invalid syntax and ensure the context is handled correctly according to the Svelte 5 documentation for `state_referenced_locally`.

#### 	import { type Snippet } from 'svelte';  
#### 	import { browser } from '$app/environment';  
#### 	import '../app.css';  
#### 	import { getMode, setMode } from './mode.svelte';  
#### 	import StatusLine from './status-line.svelte';  
#### 	import SignColumn from './sign-column.svelte';  
#### 	import { setContext } from 'svelte';  
#### 	// import { writable } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove writable import  
#### 	let { children }: { children: Snippet } = $props();  
####   
#### 	if (browser) {  
#### 		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();  
#### 		let pressedKeys = $state<string>(''); // Track pressed keys  
#### 		// const pressedKeysStore = writable(''); // Create a writable store  
####   
#### 		setContext('pressedKeys', () => pressedKeys); // Pass the state to the context  
####   
#### 		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {  
#### 			const root = document.querySelector(':root');  
#### 			const github = document.getElementById('github');  
#### 			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');  
#### 			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');  
#### 			const youtube = document.getElementById('youtube');  
#### 			const linkedin = document.getElementById('linkedin');  
#### 			const talks = document.getElementById('talks');  
#### 			const email = document.getElementById('email');  
####   
#### 			const menuItems = [  
#### 				github,  
#### 				twitter,  
#### 				twitch,  
#### 				youtube,  
#### 				linkedin,  
#### 				talks,  
#### 				email  
#### 			];  
####   
#### 			const keybinds = {  
#### 				github: 'ggh',  
#### 				twitter: 'gx',  
#### 				twitch: 'gt',  
#### 				youtube: 'gyt',  
#### 				linkedin: 'gli',  
#### 				talks: 'gct',  
#### 				email: 'gcm'  
#### 			};  
####   
#### 			const linkMap = {  
#### 				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',  
#### 				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',  
#### 				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',  
#### 				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',  
#### 				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',  
#### 				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',  
#### 				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'  
#### 			};  
####   
#### 			if (  
#### 				!root ||  
#### 				!github ||  
#### 				!twitter ||  
#### 				!twitch ||  
#### 				!youtube ||  
#### 				!linkedin ||  
#### 				!talks ||  
#### 				!email  
#### 			) {  
#### 				return;  
#### 			}  
####   
#### 			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {  
#### 				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {  
#### 					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when using j/k  
#### 					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store  
#### 					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {  
#### 						menuItems[0]?.focus();  
#### 						focusedItemIdx = 0;  
#### 						return;  
#### 					}  
####   
#### 					if (event.key === 'j') {  
#### 						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {  
#### 							return;  
#### 						}  
####   
#### 						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();  
#### 						return;  
#### 					}  
####   
#### 					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {  
#### 						return;  
#### 					}  
#### 					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();  
#### 					return;  
#### 				}  
#### 			}  
####   
#### 			if (event.key === 'i') {  
#### 				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {  
#### 					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();  
#### 				}  
#### 				setMode('INSERT');  
#### 				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering insert mode  
#### 				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store  
#### 				return;  
#### 			}  
####   
#### 			if (event.key === 'n' || event.key === 'Escape') {  
#### 				setMode('NORMAL');  
#### 				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when exiting insert mode  
#### 				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store  
####   
#### 				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {  
#### 					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();  
#### 				}  
#### 				return;  
#### 			}  
####   
#### 			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {  
#### 				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {  
#### 					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();  
#### 				}  
#### 				setMode('VISUAL');  
#### 				pressedKeys = ''; // Clear pressed keys when entering visual mode  
#### 				// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store  
#### 				return;  
#### 			}  
####   
#### 			if (getMode() === 'NORMAL' && event.key.length === 1) {  
#### 				pressedKeys += event.key;  
#### 				// pressedKeysStore.set(pressedKeys); // Update the store  
####   
#### 				const fullKeybind = Object.values(keybinds).find(  
#### 					(keybind) => keybind === pressedKeys  
#### 				);  
####   
#### 				if (fullKeybind) {  
#### 					// Navigate if full keybind is entered  
#### 					window.location.href = linkMap[fullKeybind];  
#### 					pressedKeys = ''; // Clear after navigation  
#### 					// pressedKeysStore.set(''); // Also clear the store  
#### 					return;  
#### 				}  
#### 			}  
#### 		});  
#### 	}  
####   
#### 	injectSpeedInsights();  
#### </script>  
####   
#### <div  
#### 	class="w-screen h-screen bg-ctp-base flex flex-col text-ctp-subtext0 justify-between overflow-auto"  
#### >  
#### 	<div class="flex flex-row sm:gap-4 grow">  
#### 		<SignColumn />  
#### 		{@render children()}  
#### 	</div>  
#### 	<StatusLine />  
#### </div>  
#### ```  
####   
#### **3. Modify `src/routes/+page.svelte`:**  
####   
####    - The `getContext` call should return a function that returns the string. You need to call this function to get the actual string value.  
####   
#### ```svelte  
#### // src/routes/+page.svelte  
#### <script lang="ts">  
#### 	import MainMenu from './main-menu.svelte';  
#### 	import { getContext } from 'svelte';  
#### 	// import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';  
####   
#### 	const getPressedKeys = getContext<() => string>('pressedKeys');  
#### </script>  
####   
#### <svelte:head>  
#### 	<title>dillonis.online</title>  
#### 	<meta name="description" content="Dillon Mulroy's personal website" />  
#### </svelte:head>  
####   
#### <MainMenu pressedKeys={getPressedKeys()} />  
#### ```  
####   
#### These changes remove the invalid syntax and ensure the context is handled correctly according to the Svelte 5 documentation for `state_referenced_locally`.
