<script lang="ts">
	import Ascii from './ascii.svelte';
	import {
		Github,
		LinkedinIcon,
		MailPlusIcon,
		MicVocalIcon,
		TwitchIcon,
		TwitterIcon,
		YoutubeIcon
	} from 'lucide-svelte';
  // import { get } from 'svelte/store'; // Remove get import
  import { type Writable } from 'svelte/store';

	type Props = {
		pressedKeys: string;
	};

	const { pressedKeys }: Props = $props();

  // $: pressedKeysValue = $pressedKeys;

	function highlightKeybind(keybind: string, pressedKeys: string) {
		let highlighted = '';
		for (let i = 0; i < keybind.length; i++) {
			if (i < pressedKeys.length && keybind[i] === pressedKeys[i]) {
				highlighted += `<span class="keybind-highlight">${keybind[i]}</span>`;
			} else {
				highlighted += keybind[i];
			}
		}
		return highlighted;
	}
</script>

#### Add the ability to press the keys next to the menu/items links in the main menu to go to the corresponding link. When a key is pressed Insert mode should be entered. As the user presses the corresponding keypresses the letters should be highlighted (e.g. g highlights all the g's, l - l, i -i and then goes to linked in).  				}
-				return;
 			}
 
-			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
-				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
-					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
+			// Handle starting a shortcut sequence in NORMAL mode
+			if (mode === 'NORMAL' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
+				const potentialStarters = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(event.key.toLowerCase()));
+				if (potentialStarters.length > 0) {
+					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
+						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
+						focusedItemIdx = undefined; // Clear focus
+					}
+					setMode('INSERT');
+					updateShortcutSequence(event.key.toLowerCase());
+					event.preventDefault();
+					// Check if the single key is already a full shortcut
+					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[currentShortcutSequence];
+					if (fullMatchUrl) {
+						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
+						resetShortcutSequence();
+						setMode('NORMAL');
+					}
+					return;
 				}
-				setMode('VISUAL');
-				return;
+			}
+
+			// Handle shortcut sequence typing in INSERT mode
+			if (mode === 'INSERT' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
+				const pressedKey = event.key.toLowerCase();
+				const nextSequence = currentShortcutSequence + pressedKey;
+				const potentialMatches = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(nextSequence));
+
+				if (potentialMatches.length > 0) {
+					updateShortcutSequence(pressedKey); // Append the key
+					event.preventDefault();
+
+					// Check for full match
+					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[currentShortcutSequence]; // Check updated sequence
+					if (fullMatchUrl) {
+						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
+						resetShortcutSequence();
+						setMode('NORMAL');
+					}
+				} else {
+					// Key does not extend any potential shortcut, ignore it
+					event.preventDefault();
+				}
+				return; // Handled shortcut key
+			}
+
+			// Prevent default for unhandled keys in INSERT mode (except Esc/n handled above)
+			if (mode === 'INSERT') {
+				event.preventDefault();
 			}
 		});
 	}

```

=======
			const shortcuts: Record<string, string> = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};
			const shortcutKeys = Object.keys(shortcuts);

			const mode = getMode(); // Get current mode

			// Always handle Escape/n in INSERT mode to exit
			if (mode === 'INSERT' && (event.key === 'Escape' || event.key.toLowerCase() === 'n')) {
				event.preventDefault();
				resetShortcutSequence();
				setMode('NORMAL');
				// Re-focus previously focused item if applicable
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			// Ignore modifier keys to prevent unintended behavior
			if (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey || event.altKey) {
				return;
			}

			// Ensure root element exists for mode color changes
			if (!root) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle 'i' to enter INSERT mode (only when NORMAL)
			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (mode === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
						// Optional: focusedItemIdx = undefined;
					}
					setMode('INSERT');
					resetShortcutSequence(); // Ensure sequence is reset
					event.preventDefault();
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle 'v' to enter VISUAL mode (only when NORMAL)
			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (mode === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
					}
					setMode('VISUAL');
					event.preventDefault();
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle starting a shortcut sequence in NORMAL mode
			if (mode === 'NORMAL' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
				const potentialStarters = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(event.key.toLowerCase()));
				if (potentialStarters.length > 0) {
					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
						focusedItemIdx = undefined; // Clear focus
					}
					setMode('INSERT');
					updateShortcutSequence(event.key.toLowerCase());
					event.preventDefault();
					// Check if the single key is already a full shortcut
					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[currentShortcutSequence];
					if (fullMatchUrl) {
						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
						resetShortcutSequence();
						setMode('NORMAL');
					}
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle shortcut sequence typing in INSERT mode
			if (mode === 'INSERT' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
				const pressedKey = event.key.toLowerCase();
				const nextSequence = currentShortcutSequence + pressedKey;
				const potentialMatches = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(nextSequence));

				if (potentialMatches.length > 0) {
					updateShortcutSequence(pressedKey); // Append the key
					event.preventDefault();

					// Check for full match
					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[currentShortcutSequence]; // Check updated sequence
					if (fullMatchUrl) {
						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
						resetShortcutSequence();
						setMode('NORMAL');
					}
				} else {
					// Key does not extend any potential shortcut, ignore it
					event.preventDefault();
				}
				return; // Handled shortcut key
			}

			// Prevent default for unhandled keys in INSERT mode (except Esc/n handled above)
			if (mode === 'INSERT') {
				event.preventDefault();
			}
		});
	}
>>>>>>> REPLACE

=======
			const shortcuts: Record<string, string> = {
				ggh: 'https://github.com/dmmulroy',
				gx: 'https://x.com/dillon_mulroy',
				gt: 'https://twitch.tv/dmmulroy',
				gyt: 'https://youtube.com/dmmulroy',
				gli: 'https://www.linkedin.com/in/dillon-mulroy',
				gct: 'https://dillonis.online/talks',
				gcm: 'mailto:dillon.mulroy@gmail.com'
			};
			const shortcutKeys = Object.keys(shortcuts);

			const mode = getMode(); // Get current mode

			// Always handle Escape/n in INSERT mode to exit
			if (mode === 'INSERT' && (event.key === 'Escape' || event.key.toLowerCase() === 'n')) {
				event.preventDefault();
				resetShortcutSequence();
				setMode('NORMAL');
				// Re-focus previously focused item if applicable
				if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
					menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
				}
				return;
			}

			// Ignore modifier keys to prevent unintended behavior
			if (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey || event.altKey) {
				return;
			}

			// Ensure root element exists for mode color changes
			if (!root) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle 'i' to enter INSERT mode (only when NORMAL)
			if (event.key === 'i') {
				if (mode === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
						// Optional: focusedItemIdx = undefined;
					}
					setMode('INSERT');
					resetShortcutSequence(); // Ensure sequence is reset
					event.preventDefault();
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle 'v' to enter VISUAL mode (only when NORMAL)
			if (event.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') {
				if (mode === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
					}
					setMode('VISUAL');
					event.preventDefault();
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle starting a shortcut sequence in NORMAL mode
			if (mode === 'NORMAL' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
				const potentialStarters = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(event.key.toLowerCase()));
				if (potentialStarters.length > 0) {
					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
						focusedItemIdx = undefined; // Clear focus
					}
					setMode('INSERT');
					updateShortcutSequence(event.key.toLowerCase());
					event.preventDefault();
					// Check if the single key is already a full shortcut
					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[currentShortcutSequence];
					if (fullMatchUrl) {
						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
						resetShortcutSequence();
						setMode('NORMAL');
					}
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle shortcut sequence typing in INSERT mode
			if (mode === 'INSERT' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
				const pressedKey = event.key.toLowerCase();
				const nextSequence = currentShortcutSequence + pressedKey;
				const potentialMatches = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(nextSequence));

				if (potentialMatches.length > 0) {
					updateShortcutSequence(pressedKey); // Append the key
					event.preventDefault();

					// Check for full match
					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[currentShortcutSequence]; // Check updated sequence
					if (fullMatchUrl) {
						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
						resetShortcutSequence();
						setMode('NORMAL');
					}
				} else {
					// Key does not extend any potential shortcut, ignore it
					event.preventDefault();
				}
				return; // Handled shortcut key
			}

			// Prevent default for unhandled keys in INSERT mode (except Esc/n handled above)
			if (mode === 'INSERT') {
				event.preventDefault();
			}
		});
	}
>>>>>>> REPLACE
```

Okay, Editor Engineer, it looks like we've run into a Svelte 5 constraint regarding exporting reactive state (`$state`) from modules. You cannot directly export state that is later reassigned within the same module.

Let's fix this by exporting a getter function instead.

**1. Update State Management (`src/routes/mode.svelte.ts`)**

*   Remove the direct export of `currentSequence`.
*   Add an exported getter function `getCurrentShortcutSequence`.

```diff
--- a/src/routes/mode.svelte.ts
+++ b/src/routes/mode.svelte.ts
@@ -33,8 +33,8 @@
 	}
 }
 
-// Export the state itself for reading in components
-export { currentSequence as currentShortcutSequence };
+// Export a getter function for the sequence state
+export function getCurrentShortcutSequence(): string {
+	return currentSequence;
+}
 
 // Functions to modify the sequence
 export function updateShortcutSequence(key: string): void {

```

**2. Update Layout (`src/routes/+layout.svelte`)**

*   Import `getCurrentShortcutSequence` instead of `currentShortcutSequence`.
*   Call the new getter function wherever the sequence value was previously read directly.

```diff
--- a/src/routes/+layout.svelte
+++ b/src/routes/+layout.svelte
@@ -6,7 +6,7 @@

 		getMode,
 		setMode,
-		currentShortcutSequence,
+		getCurrentShortcutSequence,
 		updateShortcutSequence,
 		resetShortcutSequence
 	} from './mode.svelte';
@@ -156,7 +156,7 @@
 					updateShortcutSequence(event.key.toLowerCase());
 					event.preventDefault();
 					// Check if the single key is already a full shortcut
-					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[currentShortcutSequence];
+					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[getCurrentShortcutSequence()];
 					if (fullMatchUrl) {
 						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
 						resetShortcutSequence();
@@ -169,14 +169,14 @@
 			// Handle shortcut sequence typing in INSERT mode
 			if (mode === 'INSERT' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
 				const pressedKey = event.key.toLowerCase();
-				const nextSequence = currentShortcutSequence + pressedKey;
+				const nextSequence = getCurrentShortcutSequence() + pressedKey;
 				const potentialMatches = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(nextSequence));
 
 				if (potentialMatches.length > 0) {
 					updateShortcutSequence(pressedKey); // Append the key
 					event.preventDefault();
 
-					// Check for full match
+					// Check for full match using the updated sequence via the getter
 					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[getCurrentShortcutSequence()]; // Check updated sequence
 					if (fullMatchUrl) {
 						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');

```

Okay, Editor Engineer, it seems the syntax I suggested for making the getter reactive within the `#each` block was incorrect. The `let` keyword cannot be used directly in the loop parameters like that.

Let's correct this using the `{@const}` tag inside the loop.

**1. Update Main Menu (`src/routes/main-menu.svelte`)**

*   Remove the `(let currentShortcutSequence = ...)` part from the `#each` parameters.
*   Inside each `#each` block, add a `{@const currentShortcutSequence = getCurrentShortcutSequence()}` tag before the `<span>` that uses it.

		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
			const github = document.getElementById('github');
			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');

				linkedin,

			if (
				!root ||
				!github ||
				!twitter ||
				!twitch ||
				!youtube ||
				!linkedin ||
				!email
			) {
				return;
			}

			if (event.key === 'j' || event.key === 'k') {
				if (getMode() === 'NORMAL') {
					if (focusedItemIdx === undefined) {
						menuItems[0]?.focus();
						focusedItemIdx = 0;
						return;
					}

					if (event.key === 'j') {
						if (focusedItemIdx === menuItems.length - 1) {
							return;
						}

						menuItems[++focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
						return;
					}

					if (focusedItemIdx === 0) {
						return;
					}
					menuItems[--focusedItemIdx]?.focus();
					return;
				}
			}

#### Backspace should remove keys from the stack for the keybinds to the right of the menu options  

Okay, Editor Engineer, let's ensure the backspace functionality correctly removes characters from the shortcut sequence.

**1. Backspace Functionality**

*   **Check `src/routes/mode.svelte.ts`:** Verify that the `removeLastShortcutChar` function is present and correctly implemented:

```typescript
export function removeLastShortcutChar(): void {
    currentSequence = currentSequence.slice(0, -1);
}
```

*   **Check `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:** Verify that the `Backspace` key is handled correctly in the `keydown` listener when in INSERT mode:

```typescript
// Handle Backspace in INSERT mode
if (mode === 'INSERT' && event.key === 'Backspace') {
    removeLastShortcutChar();
    event.preventDefault();
    return;
}
```

**Explanation:**

*   The `removeLastShortcutChar` function uses `slice(0, -1)` to create a new string that excludes the last character of the `currentSequence`.
*   The `keydown` listener checks if the mode is `INSERT` and the pressed key is `Backspace`. If both conditions are true, it calls `removeLastShortcutChar()` to update the sequence and `preventDefault()` to prevent the browser from navigating back.

If the backspace is still not working, double check that you have saved the files.

			// Handle starting a shortcut sequence in NORMAL mode
			if (mode === 'NORMAL' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
				const potentialStarters = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(event.key.toLowerCase()));
				if (potentialStarters.length > 0) {
					if (focusedItemIdx !== undefined) {
						menuItems[focusedItemIdx]?.blur();
						focusedItemIdx = undefined; // Clear focus
					}
					setMode('INSERT');
					updateShortcutSequence(event.key.toLowerCase());
					event.preventDefault();
					// Check if the single key is already a full shortcut using the getter
					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[getCurrentShortcutSequence()];
					if (fullMatchUrl) {
						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
						resetShortcutSequence();
						setMode('NORMAL');
					}
					return;
				}
			}

			// Handle shortcut sequence typing in INSERT mode
			if (mode === 'INSERT' && /^[a-z]$/i.test(event.key)) {
				const pressedKey = event.key.toLowerCase();
				const nextSequence = getCurrentShortcutSequence() + pressedKey;
				const potentialMatches = shortcutKeys.filter((s) => s.startsWith(nextSequence));

				if (potentialMatches.length > 0) {
					updateShortcutSequence(pressedKey);
					event.preventDefault();

					const fullMatchUrl = shortcuts[getCurrentShortcutSequence()];
					if (fullMatchUrl) {
						window.open(fullMatchUrl, '_blank');
						resetShortcutSequence();
						setMode('NORMAL');
					}
				} else {
					// Key does not extend any potential shortcut, ignore it
					event.preventDefault();
				}
				return; // Handled shortcut key
			}

			// Prevent default for unhandled keys in INSERT mode (except Esc/n handled above)
			if (mode === 'INSERT') {
				event.preventDefault();
			}
		});

#### pressing jj in rapid succession should also exit the current mode back to normal mode  

Okay, Editor Engineer, let's add the "jj" shortcut to exit the current mode back to normal mode.

**1. Add "jj" Shortcut Functionality**

*   **Modify `src/routes/+layout.svelte`:** Add logic to detect "jj" key presses in rapid succession and exit the current mode.

```diff
--- a/src/routes/+layout.svelte
+++ b/src/routes/+layout.svelte
@@ -21,6 +21,7 @@
 
 	if (browser) {
 		let focusedItemIdx = $state<number>();
+		let lastKeyPressTime = $state<number>(0); // Track last key press time
 
 		// Helper function to get menu items
 		function getMenuItems(): (HTMLElement | null)[] {
@@ -30,6 +31,20 @@
 
 		window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
 			const root = document.querySelector(':root');
+
+			// Check for rapid "jj" key presses
+			if (event.key === 'j' && getMode() !== 'NORMAL') {
+				const currentTime = Date.now();
+				if (currentTime - lastKeyPressTime < 200) {
+					// Rapid "jj" detected, exit insert mode
+					resetShortcutSequence();
+					setMode('NORMAL');
+					event.preventDefault();
+					return;
+				}
+				lastKeyPressTime = currentTime; // Update last key press time
+			}
+
 			const github = document.getElementById('github');
 			const twitter = document.getElementById('twitter');
 			const twitch = document.getElementById('twitch');

```

**Explanation:**

*   We introduce a `lastKeyPressTime` variable to track the time of the last key press.
*   Inside the `keydown` event listener, we check if the pressed key is "j" and the current mode is not "NORMAL".
*   If the time difference between the current key press and the last key press is less than 200 milliseconds (adjust this value as needed), we consider it a rapid "jj" and exit the current mode.
*   We call `resetShortcutSequence()` to clear any existing shortcut sequence.
*   We call `setMode('NORMAL')` to switch back to normal mode.
*   We call `event.preventDefault()` to prevent the browser from performing any default action.
*   If the key press is not a rapid "jj", we update the `lastKeyPressTime` to the current time.

**4. Consider Using a Store for `currentSequence`**

*   While the current getter/setter approach for `currentSequence` works, using a Svelte store might provide a more streamlined way to manage this reactive state, especially if other components need to react to changes in the shortcut sequence. **5. Speed Insights Trusted Dependencies**

Did you mean to match some of these actual lines from src/routes/sign-column.svelte?

```
	let signColumn: HTMLDivElement;
	let tildes = $state<string>();

	function generateTildes() {
		const { height } = signColumn.getBoundingClientRect();

		tildes = '~\n'.repeat(Math.round(height / 22));
	}

	onMount(() => {
		generateTildes();
	});
</script>

<div
	bind:this={signColumn}
	onresize={generateTildes}
	class="max-w-[44px] h-full w-[22px] pl-1 text-right
```
